Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor; et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur; et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer: par aventure i vanroit contraction; et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And these happen more often at the joints and toes in all places where there are articulations, and they are harmful blackheads, with a color like that of flesh, and without pain in many dispositions. And when squeezed very hard, the patient feels pain, but not deeply in the body; rather it is beneath the heart. It moves well in all directions, neither forwards nor backwards, nor downwards nor upwards, nor can those at joints be cut with iron, for there might be contraction. But those on the head or forehead cause a swelling on the temples.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine; et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the blackhead is small, grasp it with tweezers and cut it at its root. If it is large, suspend it on an onion, scrape it off, then scrape away the skin around it, then stitch the wound closed until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	Of large boils hanging down
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros; et en i a de petis et de mout grans; et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	Sometimes happens in bellies and not elsewhere, and is an illness called "fungus" for its appearance, and the roots are subtle, and the heads large; and there are some small and very large ones; and I saw a man who had two on his belly that were more like fungi than anything else, with no difference, white, with fine roots, cracked open, and moisture always flowing.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine; si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	I weighed them and found one to be eighteen ounces and the other six ounces. The work of the incision is such that you should observe if the patient is moist, and the color of the flesh is pale and moist with a fine root; cut it with a wide spatula, and have the fire cautery ready in your presence.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer; et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors; et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail; et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne; puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	For when cutting, there are often too many large bloodflows, and if the blood overcomes you, then hasten to use the cautery; and if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the iron incision, then take a well-made lead thread, and tie it around the flesh as we have said, and leave it for two days; then tighten it, and do not cease tightening with the lead thread until you cut through the flesh, and cut it out without struggle. And if the roots are large, there is fear in cutting itself due to the belly, but you can indeed cut half of it, then cauterize it so that it does not return; then treat the wound, ensuring that you do not cut the boil which is of dark color and poor sense and produces milk-like discharge.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	Because this is an enchanted abscess, and I will come to the treatment of cancer hereafter.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the belly swells
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit; et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	If the swelling of the belly comes from a cautery wound or a fissure of the anus, and is on the stomach and in some of the bowels, as it happens with other ruptures, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries, according to what is mentioned before, or from windiness; and if it is due to the rupture of the anus and the escape of the bowel, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and there is little pain or sensation, with various openings.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to the escape of the intestines, then it is more varied; and when you press it with your fingers, it sinks down and then returns, and sometimes it becomes hard, enlarging greatly at the entrance to the bathhouse, especially during heavy labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie; et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit; et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it's due to moisture, it is an easy thing, and you can tell clearly when you press it with your hand; it doesn't constrain at all. And if it's due to blood, then the abscesses are large and hard, and they are fixed according to a certain quantity. And if it's due to windiness, it is soft to the touch, and its appearance shows whether it's from arterial or venous blood, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	Then you must leave the treatment to [a professional].
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear about it, as I have told you in the chapter on abscesses, concerning both artery and vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude; puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine; puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz; puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine; se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre; et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit; et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier; puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi; ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit; et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And if the appearance is for the intestine or the bladder, you must command the patient to paint their anus and lie flat on their back. Then grasp all around the buttocks, then command them to lie quietly between your hands. Then move around the area that you have marked with the spatula. Then stretch half of the abscess upwards towards the large bone. Then tie it tightly with a strong thread or silk rope, ensuring the knot is secure. Then open the stretched half of the abscess on top of the ligature and insert your index finger to find the intestine. If you find it trapped by the ligature, release it and place the intestine behind the belly. And if you find the bladder, take it with the forceps and remove the excess. If the artery or vein is against you, then go carefully around, then return to your work and take two needles, and thread two strong threads through them. Insert the two needles into the area that you pierced previously in a cross shape. Then hold the abscess in four places on top of the needles, and if it breaks open, remove the needles and leave the area until it can be properly cauterized and dead flesh removed. When it is subtle and ready to cauterize, then cauterize it as we have said; and draw out the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the area as necessary, and close the wound.
dou chancre	disease
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer; et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement; et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner; ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	We have discussed in the division the similarities of cancer and how one should operate with medicines, and how to avoid the cure of iron. And we say cancer that appears in the marrow, and great caution is needed in its treatment. The ancients said that when cancers are in a place where they can be cut out like those found on the breasts, buttocks, and similar places, all should be removed at the beginning; but when they are large and old, one must not approach them because none have ever been healed from them, nor has anyone before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire; puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige; puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier; et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the operation, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, involves purging the patient of black bile once; then make them vomit if they show signs of repletion, then prepare the patient well for the operation. Then cut out your oncines or cancer and the skin all around it, and remove it all without leaving anything behind. Let the blood flow freely, and press the wound well with your hand or some other thing. If the bleeding makes your incision difficult due to an artery or vein, cauterize it until the bleeding stops; then treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
de ydropisie	Hydropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer: lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	We have already discussed in the division the similarities of dropsy, and how the accumulation of water is formed, and the signs of each type, and the treatment that is done with medicines, and that which is treated by iron: only eclites is mentioned; and one should not use iron in these two types: namely tympanites and yposarche, for they are deadly things; therefore when you treat this type of dropsy called "eclites" with medicines, and the cure does not help, then examine if the patient is weak, or if they have another illness besides dropsy, such as wind and bloating and similar things; do not use iron here, for there is doubt; and if you see that the patient has strong virtue, and they have no other illness besides dropsy alone, and they are neither too young nor too old, then you should act thus: lift the patient upright onto your hands, and the assistants press the belly outward, pushing the water towards the lowest part of the chest, then take the spatumile espinous in this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let it be cut in two.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier; puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu; puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	Then pierce it thus: do not cut so deeply that it reaches the intestines when you insert it, and do not let it bleed. Then observe if the dropsy has entered near the intestines: if so, make an incision three finger widths below the navel on the right side; if it is due to liver disease, make the incision to the left of the navel; if it is from mucus, make it on the right side. Ensure that the patient does not lie on the incision so that the superfluities do not flow into this weak area. Then pierce all the skin with the instrument and insert it, and raise your hand so that the spatula lies between the skin and the syfac, as when skinning, to the depth of one fingernail or about that amount. Then pierce the syfac until the spatula reaches the empty space, which is the location of water, then draw it out and insert this instrument...
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus; et II d’autre part, et I d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	And it is like a thin silver chain, and it is of arrow or lightweight steel, and there is a small hole in its lower part; and on one side, three holes; and two on another side, and one more; and the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that scribes use to cut feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort; mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit; fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	And at the head above is the alembic, so that when the tool reaches the water, it should then stop on the tool. Empty out one-half or one-third of it now, for if you empty more than is necessary at this time, perhaps the patient may die from the spirit of the weapon dissolving in him, or he may fall unconscious, or approach death; but empty according to its quantity and strength, and according to what the condition of the patient's pulse signifies. Then draw out the tool and hold back the water, which is held back by the heart stopping up the hole that is on the face, as I have spoken of it, which you should pierce in this manner; then recommence the tool on another day if you see the patient enduring these things, and draw out a little quantity of water. Do this several days, but guard yourself so that not too much water remains but only a drop.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave much water on him, then treat with hot burial or sand, and with much sweat or bath and sun exposure, and apply a dye to drink; and treat with drying medicines until he is sound, and cauterize on the stomach and liver and spleen after the extraction of the water, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	Of the stopping of the erection
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	No child is born without an opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If necessary, it should be pierced at once with a very fine spatula according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	then place a thin cloth plug of lead, and tie it and hold it thus for 3 or 4 days. When it wants to urinate, remove the plug, let it urinate, and then replace it. And perhaps it may not be necessary, because urine that comes forth does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose wound is small, let him apply the cloth of lead, as we have said; thus it will widen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	Those whose wounds are not in their proper place are wounded, for some are born with the opening at the head of the penis, which prevents them from urinating before they lift their penis upwards; and they cannot enter due to the fact that matter cannot reach the bladder, and this is a serious disease.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the manner of this procedure is that the patient lies on his back, then raise the head of the penis and cut it like the edge of a feather, so that the opening falls in the middle as it should; and beware of bleeding that often occurs there, and if it does happen, stop it with something that stops blood, and heal the wound until it is healthy.
des pustules de la verge	warts of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times these warts appear on the penis, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh; and there are malignant and non-malignant ones; therefore you must grasp them with a sharp lancet, cut them all around, then cleanse them with Egyptian ointment, then cure them with soft ointment until they are healthy.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the wound is malignant, of foul color and foul smelling, then you must bring fire cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	When you've cut it out and if the wound is deep on the penis, with part inside the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the wound that's inside; and when it's united, then treat the one outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	For if you treat them together, the head of the penis is not secure and may be pierced, leading to blackness and corruption in the glans and scrotum; thus all that is black and corrupted should be cut away, then apply a poultice made of honey, flour, and pomegranate peel mixed with sesame seeds. Then treat it with other remedies until it's healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is profuse bleeding, then bring the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars; et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	The cautery helps with two conditions together: namely, bleeding and corruption. And if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, then you should insert a lead pipe into the glans so that the patient can piss through it; and when the skin at the tip of the penis is tense (this happens to those who have not been circumcised, or due to wound or abscess), then you must burn it with the heated spoon until the ligaments are severed and the head of the penis is released on all sides. If it's difficult to separate them, then burn a little from the tip of the penis and skin with the spatula; then gently separate them, and put a thin linen cloth moistened in cold water between them.
de la circoncision	Circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not the same as other wounds in terms of continuity; nevertheless, when we perform this operation by choice, especially on children, it is necessary to do our best work and make it as easy as possible to heal.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not practice circumcision on their sons, as it was not part of their law, and we only have knowledge of what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For the most part, masters and surgeons who perform circumcision around the glans take off too much skin and flesh, even down to the novacule; thus the heart falters because there are two layers of skin, and sometimes one layer is cut while the other remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Otherwise, the wound opens up again and causes double pain. During cleaning, the glans is not securely held by the tip of the member; sometimes the iron slips while cleaning the foreskin and ruins the operation. Many times wounds heal without needing further cleaning, as I have seen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the process of filing which is performed on horses' hooves throughout their entire length with fine wire, I have found the benefit of experience.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues; puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien; et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge; puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you press your hand, if you file evenly throughout the entire length of time; but let the wire be well wrapped around the hide; and the manner of the first operation should be such that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the wire around the verge. Then let him enjoy all the ways that you can; then have him stand upright between your hands, and put the file between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the tools. Then put your hand on the verge and blow in the heart, and draw it up until the head of the verge is inside. Then clean it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then mark the spot with a double thread, then tie it below the knot at the other joint. Then hold it with both hands by the second knot on the pouch and index finger, and cut between the two joints, then raise the heart quickly and draw out the head of the verge. Then let the blood flow well from the pouch to the pouch, for this is the medicine. Then put powder on it and on the powder a cloth glued with an egg yolk tempered with rose water, cooked together with good fresh rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, and treat him again until he is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The form of the cauterizing force is thus: The two heads should be thin and sharp; they should also be as large as a hazelnut evenly.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	The mistake in cauterizing is when the heart inside flees from the incision. Therefore, you must stretch it with your thumbnail before the place forms an abscess; cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your thumbnail, then use tongs to do so.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it lasts for three days, and the part below the vein is swollen, then let it be until the swelling has decreased and the scab is lightly scraped off; cut it as much as you can move it, but take care not to harm the vein itself.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore, treat the place of sudden wound with powder, as we have said in treating powders. If you cut too deeply and it goes upwards, then there will be no harm; treat it accordingly until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	Retention of urine is due to the blocking of stone, or frozen blood, or bowel, or flesh newly grown, or similar things, which we have spoken of in the division. And if urine is not released, and you see that retention is caused by a stone located at the neck of the bladder, then it is necessary for the patient to kneel on their knees; and place their feet on their back, and extend their belly from the part above the back, and the patient holds themselves up as much as they can. And then the neck of the bladder is forced open to expel the stone above, so that urine is released. And if it does not come out, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must perform extraction using all the instruments called "syringe", of which this is the form: and it should be made of thin, lightweight silver, like a bird's feather; and the tube should be one-and-a-half palms long, and thin at the end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the manner of urine discharge is thus: Take a doubled thread and tie it to the head of a wool or cotton pouch, then insert the thread's head into the syringe. Cut off excess wool from the pouch and place it up to the syringe's mouth. Then anoint the syringe with oil, butter, or egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a chair. Anoint their bladder and penis with moistened olive oil and cold water. Gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the belly. Insert the syringe further until the patient feels urine coming out from the empty space, which may not happen if the passage is twisted. Then slowly pull out the thread along with the wool pouch and allow the urine to follow the wool. Remove the thread and let the urine flow. Repeat the process with the syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient feels relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	Of bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When you see that blood comes into the bladder or putrefaction is gathered there, and you observe water or medicine being distilled onto it, then do all the instruments called "clepsydras," which are shaped thus:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed and has III openings: II on one side, and I on the other, as you see. The raised places are so that medicine can fit well without additional help, allowing moisture to be drawn out and inserted when needed. When you see your medicines flowing into the bladder, place the head of the catheter in the moisture, and draw with the tube that is inside it. Then put the moisture back into the catheter and strongly push the tube back in; then the moisture will enter and reach the bladder now, so the patient can feel it. And this is the shape of the delicate catheter used to irrigate the bladder:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is of silver or lead, and the head is higher; and below it falls to the breast; then take a sheep's bladder and fill it with moisture that you will use for irrigation, then tie it between the two breasts firmly with a doubled thread, and warm this moisture on the fire; then insert the head of the irrigation device into the penis, then squeeze your hand on the bladder until all the moisture reaches the bladder; and if you do not have a bladder, then take a piece of parchment, and make a circle from it, and pierce it evenly around; then insert a strong thread into these holes, then assemble the circle like you would an awl, and put within it what you will use for oil and moisture and water, and tie it onto the instrument; and do as you have done with the bladder, by squeezing your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	Of stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already said in the division the ways of stone and their extraction together with medications; and we have spoken about the difference between a stone embedded in the kidneys and all its signs, and in which stones one should operate by cutting; and concerning the bladder and the penis; and I will tell you this clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that stones embedded in the bladder occur more often in children, and this is a sign that urine comes out of the bladder like water in its fineness; and it opens clearly and the patient feels pain in his penis, and he urinates many times and then becomes constipated; and the foundation of most of these cases is weakness; and healing is easy for children until they are four years old, but difficult for the elderly, and it is moderate for those who are between youth and old age; and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, first it is necessary to cleanse the patient through a clyster, to draw out all the waste that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For sometimes it obstructs the passage of urine.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet, and raise them up and move them below, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it may fall from its high position; then have him sit between your hands prepared, and his hands should be under his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downward; then search for it and touch it inside; if you feel the stone in the space, now hasten to cut on the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not fall when touched from above, then moisten your index finger with oil of the left hand, if the patient is a child, or your middle finger, if the patient is fully grown; and insert it into his anus, search for the stone, and when you feel it on your finger, move it to the neck of the bladder; then press on your finger and push it out where you see to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And command the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and tell him to stretch out his right hand with the thighs upward, and remove the skin that is under the thighs in the part where you make the cut; then place the scalpel cutting downwards.
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And make the incision between what is between the thighs and the fundament, not in the middle but on the left side of the buttock; let it be straight on the stone, with your thumb always on the fundament, and cut across so that it is wide outside and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone; sometimes press the thumb that is on the fundament so that it comes out without effort. Know that there are stones with angles and edges: these are difficult to remove. And there are those that are smooth, round like a hazelnut, from which removal is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	Therefore for those that have angles and edges, make the incision larger. And if it does not come out, then you must remove it with forceps which are like a chisel at the head, to pull out the stone so that it does not escape; or insert a subtle curved instrument underneath. And if you cannot catch it this way, then widen the hole and if blood flows, stop it with vitriol. And if there is more than one stone, first put the largest one into the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, then pull it out, and afterwards remove the smaller ones if there are more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be opened with a larger cut.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	And there are two things that may happen to the patient: either he dies, or urine begins to flow continuously from the wound which cannot be closed. But nevertheless, you should try your best to pull out the stone with forceps, piece by piece; and once you have completed your task, cover the wound with incense, aloe, and dragon's blood, then bandage it tightly. Then place a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine or oil and rosewater and cold water on top to cool the inflamed abscess. Then bind the patient's neck and do not untie the bandage for three days.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you unbind it, rinse the wound very well with oil and water, then treat it with ointment of diaphoretic and ointment of basilicon until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if an abscess appears in the wound and corrosions, and coagulations of blood in the bladder, causing urine retention which is known to occur in such a way that it flows out without warning with urine: then boil your two fingers over the wound, and remove that blood, for if it remains there it will corrupt the bladder and harm it; then wash the wound with water and salt and silk, and aid him in every way you know until he is healed; and it is necessary that whenever you treat him, you bind his two thighs together, and apply medicine to the location.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small and it is in the passage of the penis and stuck inside, and urine cannot flow out; then perform the treatment that I mentioned earlier, cutting it many times until it is pierced through by this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proven this to be true.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take an iron rod according to this form and have three spikes forged into one piece of wood:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take thread and wrap it around the stalk beneath the stone so that it cannot retreat into the bladder. Then insert the probe lightly into the stalk until it reaches the stone; then turn the probe in your hand against the stone gently, repeatedly until you can pierce the stone from the other side. Then urine will soon come forth, then press your hand on what remains of the stone inside the stalk.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is soon broken and exits with the urine, then the patient is healed. And if you cannot do this for any reason that hinders it, then tie one thread beneath the stone and another above it, then make an incision in the stalk at the stone between the two threads, then remove it forth and untie the knot, and cleanse the congealed blood that is in the wound; and treat it until it is healthy.
de la piere des femmes	Of the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It happens rarely that a stone enters into women, and if it does happen sometimes, the cure is difficult, and there are three reasons for this: one is that by chance the woman is a virgin; another is that it is hard to find a woman who knows how to expose herself to physicians, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	The third manner is such that perhaps one cannot find a woman well-versed in this art of hands; and the fourth manner is that the stone of the woman is more hidden than that of the man, therefore a deeper cut must be made, and there is great fear involved. If you are unable to find such a woman, then you must take a young, skilled midwife, and if one cannot be found, then search for a subtle and wise physician; present her with a wise woman who knows about women's lives or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to perform the examination of the stone according to your commands. Pay close attention to whether the woman is a virgin: she must place her hand on the fundament and search for the stone; if she finds it, she should press it down with her hand, and then command her to place her hand on the patient's womb and seek and press her left hand firmly on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If she finds it, she must move it little by little from the entrance of the bladder until she reaches the root of the thigh; then cut on the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the penis, where it has moved and can be felt; and do not move her hand above or below the stone, making the incision first small; then insert the probe into the incision if you feel the stone so close to the wound that the stone can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones: namely, small and large, sharp and smooth, long and round, and those with roots.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	and recognize the similarities to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood flows abundantly, then put powdered vitriol in place and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your work until the stone is removed, having tools ready as I have told you for extracting stones from men to aid you in your task; and if blood flows profusely and it is from the artery that was cut, then apply powder on the wound and compress with linen and bandages, and do not attempt this again, leaving the stone alone without pulling it out lest by chance the patient dies; then dress the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat from the blood is perceived, and the place becomes porous, then it returns to your task, until the stone is burning.
de hernie carnouse	of soft tissue hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	RamiCes aqueous is nothing other than an assembly of moisture or white amniotic fluid that is beneath the skin of the kidneys, containing the egg; and it is called 'amniotic' fluid, sometimes properly found in the wall of the egg itself, so one might think it is another egg. This is the skin of the kidney between the white amniotic fluid that we have spoken about; and this does not happen unless there is a lack.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this hernia comes from weakness in the kidneys, causing expansion of that material.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from percussion on the kidneys, and this moisture has many colors: either declining towards jaundice, or without redness, or black, or white watery fluid; these are signs to recognize this assembly. For if it is the white amniotic fluid that we have spoken about, then the swelling is round like an egg shape, and long like a figure of an egg, and it does not open the kidneys because it has moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if there is moisture in the proper cloth, then the abscess is ripe with one part of the egg, and therefore it is believed to be another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the thighs and the white fat, it can be felt well; hence when you see the color of the moisture, try it on all the intrusive squares, from which its shape is known beforehand.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	Therefore, based on what comes after the insertion, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we open it with iron, the patient must be in a sitting position according to his ability and the fullness of his body; then have him lie on his back on something slightly raised, and put many cloths underneath him. Then sit on his left side, and instruct the minister to sit on the right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs of the lower abdomen. Then take the spatula, and cut the skin of the lower abdomen along the long axis near the navel, making a straight incision through the skin down to the white fat. Then carefully scrape off the fat according to your ability; then pierce the fat full of water with one large hole, and remove all the water, and then put on your gloves, and lift the fat upwards; and do not touch the ribcage of the lower abdomen, but only the fat itself. Cut away all or in pieces the surrounding fat carefully, so that if you do not cut it cleanly, the water will return. And if the egg slips out during your work, put it back in its place once you have completed the work on the fat. Then stitch up the two parts of the ribcage with one suture, then treat it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the egg corrupted by other disease, then you must tie the vessels that are suspended, doubting the flow of blood; then cut the skin around the entire suspension, and remove the egg, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And if water is gathered in two parts together, know that these are two branches; cut the other part equally as you did the first one; then squeeze out the blood and place moist wool in rose oil on the wound. Then place moist wool in wine and oil over both incisions, cover with doubled cloth, and tie it all according to this method.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two cloths and fill them with wool according to this form, and sew them together at the waist of the breeches. Place one end on the buttocks up to the back, and the other at the wrist area. Then bring the two ends together over the hips, and gather all the restraint around the loop of the breeches. Sometimes this branch is treated with cautery instead of iron cutting; take a sharp scalpel cautery and cut the skin of the incisions. Heat it as we have said until the white bubble containing the water is exposed. Then use the cautery according to this form, pierce that bubble several times, and burn it with this sharp hot cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And cut in all ways that you can, until you strip it bare; and ensure that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this work is more beneficial; and move carefully to avoid blood loss, and move slowly with cutting works; and if anything goes against you, whether it's a boil or blood flow or something else, then treat what goes against you according to what is said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is afraid and does not want to undergo this procedure due to its horror, then perform a drainage, as I tell you. And when you are certain by the signs we have discussed that abscess water is present there, then make the patient sit on an elevated seat; pierce the boil at its lowest part with the entire spatula wide open, and insert the drainage tube along the length of the body; let the hole be large enough so that all the water flows out freely. Then place cotton on the spot and tie it, and leave it to allow the remaining water to flow out, then treat the wound until it is healed. And if the linen cloth does not allow the water to flow out from the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat hydrocephalic water, whose form is mentioned earlier. Then widen the hole in the wound, and know that the water returns and collects again after six months or so around it. And when it collects as before, then the patient will pass their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	Concerning the boil on the testicles.
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	It should be known that in the cutting of this vein there is great danger and many dispositions (preconditions), therefore it seems to me that it would be better if it were left alone; and I will tell you about the procedure and similar cases of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I say then that many boils come upon the body, especially on the testicles; and this happens in many cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is to know by acid and bitter fluid that is spread upon the testicles, or from an injury; and the color of the boil is according to the color of the body; and it does not cause pain, yet it is a serious boil. Sometimes there are several serious boils that are pale and white in color, and sometimes they come from an artery, or from swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is from an artery, it is known by the hot and hard boil that you feel when pressing with your two fingers; and you should not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	He who is made from swollen veins is recognized by his arrangement at the expression of the touch of the toes, and can well make the cut on this kind of ulcer, and on others; but you should strike the heart of the boil first, then raise the egg up high, and wipe the white surface off, and deliver the suspender from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the egg is already filled with these veins that have been born, then you must pierce and cut the egg; but if it is on the surface or within those in the vessels, then you must remove all of this fat, and roundly cut it.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the flesh is in the back area, then you must cut all of it out, and remove the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your operations are complete, dress the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	Of the boil on the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is a boil wrapped in an envelope resembling a bunch of grapes, with softening of the testicles, and the patient cries out when he walks; and the treatment of this disease is quite frightening as the one mentioned before, nevertheless we will tell you its workings according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	You must have the patient sit on a raised seat, then place the suspensory ligament of the testicles below your two fingers, close to the penis, and hold it gently; then cut through the skin wide and deep with a sharp scalpel, until the vessels are exposed, and then scrape away from each side, as we have described for extracting temporal arteries; then insert a needle with a double thread where the vein first appeared, and tie it at the first location where the vein came out, and tie it again at the other end; then cut midway straight along the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture; then treat the wound like others where an arrow has been removed, so that no vessels are left to nourish one of the testicles; for otherwise there will be no harm, but if all the vessels become filled with blood, then the testicles must be drawn from all vessels; so that the seed does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry up and cannot help.
de la routure dou syfac	From the rupture of a hernia
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The occurrence of this hernia is caused by the rupture that comes from the scrotum, or the extension on the abdomen in the region of the groin, whereby the intestines descend from that rupture to one of the testicles; and this rupture occurs either in the scrotum or in the extension of it, and these two types come about from many causes: either from a blow, or a jump, or lifting heavy weights, or similar things. And when it is an extension of the scrotum, the sign is that it happens little by little over a long period of time, and does not happen suddenly; and the swelling is even all the way to the base, because the scrotum presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the sign when it is a rupture of the scrotum is that it suddenly brings pain at the beginning, and there are diverse swellings appearing underneath the skin near by, and this is due to the exit of the intestines and the body passing through the opening of the scrotum.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the serpent, and are retained within, causing great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these cauteries with fire there is fear, therefore one must avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	And the manner of this operation is as follows: instruct the patient to put his hand inside the wound if he can reach it; then press on his neck between your hands and lift his thighs. Then raise the heart upwards, cut all the long hair off the scrotum. Then insert cloths into the groin according to what you need to open the wound so that the testicle may come out. Then scrape away the skin of the scrotum until the tough white scrotum is exposed on all sides. Then put your right index finger inside the scrotum, between the two layers of skin and behind the testicle. Then move your right hand inside the scrotum and raise the tough white scrotum with your left hand, pulling the testicle towards the groin. Instruct the assistant to hold the testicle upwards and loosen what is behind it. Search with both hands if there is any intestine wrapped around the tough white scrotum, and if you find anything, put it back inside the abdomen. Then take a needle with thick thread made of silk threads, insert it into the rear part of the scrotum after the testicle. Cut off the excess thread so that there are four strands left. Then tie them together in a cross shape and secure the tough scrotum using two knots. Then wrap the thread ends and tie them securely with two knots to prevent any vessel that nourishes it from entering or infection from coming inside. Again, place the knot according to the first one along two fingers away from the scrotum. After these two knots leave some slack in the scrotum underneath the testicle. Then cut into the part below the skin of the scrotum until blood flows and the intestine is visible as described earlier. Then bring moistened wool soaked in oil and put it on the wound, and apply the ligature that was mentioned before.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the whites of the eyes are cauterized, as we have mentioned, after incision due to fear of blood flow.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	And this happens often, leaving the thread hanging until it falls by itself. And if it takes too long to fall, let it be raised with warm water and place over what we have mentioned until it falls. Then treat the wound with another remedy until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	I never saw anyone dare to perform this surgery using iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the ancients said that it is done like the hernia that is together there, in such a way that you tie the lips after cutting lightly below, then cut in between and treat the wound with what opens until the lips fall off. Then heal it as we have said until it is healthy.
